   <div id="content">
    <div class="post singlepost">
     <h2 class="posttitle">
      <a href="http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/2012/10/26/blue-cheese-popover-muffins-recipe-harry-and-david-giveaway/" rel="bookmark">
       Blue Cheese Popover Muffins {Harry and David giveaway}
      </a>
     </h2>
     <div class="postmeta">
      <em>
       posted on
      </em>
      October 26, 2012
      <em>
       by
      </em>
      Brenda
     </div>
     <p>
      <a href="http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/10/600afd_X_IMG_9664_blue-cheese-popover-muffins-copy.jpg">
       <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-7843" height="401" src="http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/10/600afd_X_IMG_9664_blue-cheese-popover-muffins-copy.jpg" title="blue cheese popover muffins - a farmgirl's dabbles" width="600"/>
      </a>
     </p>
     <p>
      Popovers are one of my all time favorite luxuries. When served hot and steaming, with a shmear of creamy butter or sweetened
      <a href="http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/2010/10/18/cinnamon-honey-butter/" target="_blank" title="Cinnamon Honey Butter">
       cinnamon honey butter
      </a>
      I beg you to find me anything more wonderful and comforting. And the best part? They are incredibly easy to make! Heres my favorite no-fail recipe for basic
      <a href="http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/2010/10/04/popovers/" target="_blank" title="Popovers">
       popovers
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <p>
      A few weeks ago, while we were enjoying a
      <a href="http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/2011/09/30/how-we-grill-steak-plus-blue-cheese-walnut-butter/" target="_blank" title="grilled steak">
       perfectly grilled steak
      </a>
      , I wanted to reach for a popover and a hunk of blue cheese. But, alas, nobody had thought of adding those details to our menu. Nobody, as in me.
     </p>
     <p>
      And then, after enjoying quite a lot of fabulous
      <a href="http://www.roguecreamery.com/store/category/2/11/Blues/" target="_blank" title="Rogue Creamery blue cheese">
       Rogue Creamery
      </a>
      blue cheese
      <a href="http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/2012/10/19/harry-and-david-beautiful-southern-oregon/" target="_blank" title="my visit to Harry and David">
       while visiting Harry and David
      </a>
      in Oregon recently, I suddenly had all kinds of inspiration to incorporate more blue cheese in my diet. Trust me, that cheese is something you NEED to try!
      <em>
       (And if you scroll on down to the end of this post, you can enter to
       <strong>
        WIN
       </strong>
       some!)
      </em>
     </p>
     <p>
      So these
      <span style="color: #c3151e;">
       <strong>
        Blue Cheese Popover Muffins
       </strong>
      </span>
      were born. Theyre baked in a regular muffin pan, so theres no need to run out and buy a special popover pan
      <em>
       (although I highly recommend a popover pan in your cupboard!)
      </em>
      . These popover muffins dont rise and pop over the top of the cup like traditional popovers do, but they are moist, eggy, and completely delicious, just the same. With a crumbling of creamy salty blue cheese and a generous sprinkling of freshly ground black pepper, theyre just the perfect detail to add to your next grilled steak meal.
     </p>
     <p>
      <a href="http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/10/600afd_X_IMG_9632_blue-cheese-popover-muffins.jpg">
       <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-7842" height="364" src="http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/10/600afd_X_IMG_9632_blue-cheese-popover-muffins.jpg" title="blue cheese popover muffins - a farmgirl's dabbles" width="600"/>
      </a>
     </p>
     <p>
     </p>
     <div class="zlrecipe-container-border" id="zlrecipe-container-93">
      <div class="serif zlrecipe" id="zlrecipe-container" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Recipe">
       <div id="zlrecipe-innerdiv">
        <div class="item b-b">
         <div class="zlrecipe-print-link fl-r">
          <a class="butn-link" href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="zlrPrint('zlrecipe-container-93', 'http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/wp-content/plugins/ziplist-recipe-plugin/'); return false" title="Print this recipe">
           Print
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="zl-recipe-link fl-r zl-rmvd" id="zl-recipe-link-93">
         </div>
         <div class="b-b h-1 strong" id="zlrecipe-title" itemprop="name">
          Blue Cheese Popover Muffins
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="zlmeta zlclear">
         <div class="fl-l width-50">
         </div>
         <div class="fl-l width-50">
          <p id="zlrecipe-yield">
           Yield:
           <span itemprop="recipeYield">
            10 popover muffins
           </span>
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="zlclear">
         </div>
        </div>
        <p class="h-4 strong" id="zlrecipe-ingredients">
         Ingredients
        </p>
        <ul id="zlrecipe-ingredients-list">
         <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-0" itemprop="ingredients">
          2 large eggs
         </li>
         <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-1" itemprop="ingredients">
          1 c. milk
         </li>
         <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-2" itemprop="ingredients">
          1 c. all-purpose flour
         </li>
         <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-3" itemprop="ingredients">
          1/2 tsp. salt
         </li>
         <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-4" itemprop="ingredients">
          3 oz. blue cheese, crumbled
         </li>
         <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-5" itemprop="ingredients">
          freshly ground black pepper
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p class="h-4 strong" id="zlrecipe-instructions">
         Preparation
        </p>
        <span class="instructions" id="zlrecipe-instructions-list">
         <p class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-0" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
          Preheat oven to 450. Generously spray a regular size muffin pan with cooking spray and set aside.
         </p>
         <p class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-1" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
          In a medium bowl, whisk eggs and milk slightly. Add flour and salt and briskly stir to incorporate. Do not overbeat. The batter will be slightly lumpy. Pour batter into 10 muffin cups, dividing batter evenly. Add blue cheese to individual muffin cups, dividing cheese evenly. With the back of a spoon, lightly dunk the cheese under the batter. Sprinkle top of batter generously with freshly ground black pepper. Bake 15 minutes. No peeking! Keep that oven door shut and the heat inside! Decrease oven temperature to 350 and bake 12 to 15 minutes longer, until deep golden brown. Immediately remove popover muffins from cups. If they stick a bit, just use a knife to circle around the edges of the individual cups.
         </p>
         <p class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-2" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
          These are best when eaten fresh and hot, with butter.
         </p>
        </span>
        <p class="h-4 strong" id="zlrecipe-notes">
         Source
        </p>
        <div id="zlrecipe-notes-list">
         <p class="notes">
          Adapted from
          <a href="http://www.afarmgirlsdabbles.com/2010/10/04/popovers/" target="_blank">
           my favorite popover recipe
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="ziplist-recipe-plugin" style="display: none;">
         3.1
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4>
      Im linking up with:
     </h4>
     <ul>
      <li>
       Cheryl at
       <strong>
        TidyMom
       </strong>

       <a href="http://tidymom.net/2012/monster-munch-popcorn/" target="_blank" title="TidyMom - I'm Lovin' It">

       </a>

      I have GREAT news, guys!
     </p>
     <p>
      Harry and David has generously offered a
      <a href="http://www.harryanddavid.com/h/fruit-gift/fruit-and-cheese-gift-baskets/3114" target="_blank" title="Rogue Valley Gift Box from Harry and David">

      </a>
      to one very lucky
      <em>
       a farmgirls dabbles
      </em>
      reader!
     </p>
     <p>
      This gift box contains deliciousness from the Rogue Valley of southern Oregon. There are 6 sweet and juicy Royal Riviera Pears, hand picked from the Harry and David orchards, plus a variety of delectable blue cheese from the local Rogue Creamery.
